I understand the complains but anyone saying that the remake of resident evil 2 was shorter than the original are just moronic. The average time it took to beat was 6-1/2 Hours and that's someone who was a game veteran. Understand that in 1998 games were not at all what they are today and so the idea of taking time to find key items and explore in weird areas or secret locations was a new system to most. So the remake of re2 is 8ish hours if you just do the main quests and don't diverge at all. The average player is about 30hrs. Re3 on the other hand was a joke but looking into it, this was not their priority and was being developed alongside re2 remake and that is the fault of capcom, they royally f*cked up. But supposedly this has been in development for years and, to most, is considered *the best* Resident Evil. I'm optomistic but there is the possibility they'll release another RE3, but I doubt it. Maybe got cocky with RE2 release and rushed the 3rd, but just hopeful they learned their mistakes and keep it as is - if not, add more content - and do is another RE2.
